East</a></td></tr><tr class="mergedrow"><th scope="row" class="infobox-label"><a href="/wiki/Firefighting" title="Firefighting">Fire and Rescue</a></th><td class="infobox-data"><a />.uk</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Newcastle upon Tyne</b> (<span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="/nj/: &#39;n&#39; in &#39;new&#39;">nj</span><span title="/u\xcb\x90/: &#39;oo&#39; in &#39;goose&#39;">u\xcb\x90</span><span title="&#39;k&#39; in &#39;kind&#39;">k</span><span title="/\xc9\x91\xcb\x90/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;father&#39;">\xc9\x91\xcb\x90</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/\xc9\x99l/: &#39;le&#39; in &#39;bottle&#39;">\xc9\x99l</span></span>/</a></span></span>, <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><small>locally </small><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/nj/: &#39;n&#39; in &#39;new&#39;">nj</span><span title="/u\xcb\x90/: &#39;oo&#39; in &#39;goose&#39;">u\xcb\x90</span><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="&#39;k&#39; in &#39;kind&#39;">k</span><span title="/\xc3\xa6/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;bad&#39;">\xc3\xa6</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/\xc9\x99l/: &#39;le&#39; in &#39;bottle&#39;">\xc9\x99l</span></span>/</a></span>&#32;<span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:En-uk-NewcastleUponTyne(ShortA).ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/18/En-uk-NewcastleUponTyne%28ShortA%29.ogg" class="internal" title="En-uk-NewcastleUponTyne(ShortA).ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span></span>),<sup id="cite_ref-Wells2008_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wells2008-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> often simply <b>Newcastle</b>, is the most populous <a href="/wiki/City_status_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="City status in the United Kingdom">city</a> and <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_borough" title="Metropolitan borough">metropolitan borough</a> in <a href="/wiki/North_East_England" title="North East England">North East England</a>. It forms the core of the <a href="/wiki/Tyneside" title="Tyneside">Tyneside</a> <a href="/wiki/Conurbation" title="Conurbation">conurbation</a>, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_urban_areas_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="List of urban areas in the United Kingdom">eighth most populous</a> urban area in the United Kingdom. The city is situated on the <a href="/wiki/River_Tyne" title="River Tyne">River Tyne</a>\'s northern bank, approximately 8.5&#160;mi (13.7&#160;km) from the <a href="/wiki/North_Sea" title="North Sea">North Sea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> \n</p><p>Newcastle developed around a <a href="/wiki/Roman_Empire" title="Roman Empire">Roman</a> settlement called <a href="/wiki/Pons_Aelius" title="Pons Aelius">Pons Aelius</a><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> and the settlement later took the name of <a href="/wiki/The_Castle,_Newcastle" title="The Castle, Newcastle">a castle built in 1080</a> by <a href="/wiki/William_the_Conqueror" title="William the Conqueror">William the Conqueror</a>\'s eldest son, <a href="/wiki/Robert_Curthose" title="Robert Curthose">Robert Curthose</a>. \n</p><p>Historically, Newcastle\'s economy was dependant on its port. In particular, its status as one of the world\'s largest <a href="/wiki/Ship_building" class="mw-redirect" title="Ship building">ship building</a> and repair centres.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> \n</p><p>Today, the city\'s economy is diverse with major economic output in science, finance, retail, education, tourism, and nightlife. Newcastle is one of the UK <a href="/wiki/Core_Cities_Group" title="Core Cities Group">Core Cities</a>, as well as part of the <a href="/wiki/Eurocities" title="Eurocities">Eurocities</a> network.<sup id="cite_ref-coreCity_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-coreCity-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-euroCity2_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-euroCity2-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-euroCity_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-euroCity-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Famous landmarks in Newcastle include the <a href="/wiki/Tyne_Bridge" title="Tyne Bridge">Tyne Bridge</a>; the <a href="/wiki/Swing_Bridge,_River_Tyne" title="Swing Bridge, River Tyne">Swing Bridge</a>; the <a href="/wiki/Gateshead_Millennium_Bridge" title="Gateshead Millennium Bridge">Millennium Bridge</a>; <a href="/wiki/The_Castle,_Newcastle" title="The Castle, Newcastle">Newcastle Castle</a>; <a href="/wiki/Grey%27s_Monument" title="Grey&#39;s Monument">Grey\'s Monument</a>; and the <a href="/wiki/Theatre_Royal,_Newcastle" title="Theatre Royal, Newcastle">Theatre Royal</a>. Culturally, Newcastle is famed for its <a href="#Nightlife">nightlife</a>; bakery chain <a href="/wiki/Greggs" title="Greggs">Greggs</a>; television personalities <a href="/wiki/Ant_%26_Dec" title="Ant &amp; Dec">Ant &amp; Dec</a>; the <a href="/wiki/Great_North_Run" title="Great North Run">Great North Run</a> half-marathon; and <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_Football_Club" class="mw-redirect" title="Newcastle United Football Club">Newcastle United Football Club</a>. \n</p><p>Newcastle was part of the county of <a href="/wiki/Northumberland" title="Northumberland">Northumberland</a> until 1400 when it became a <a href="/wiki/County_of_itself" class="mw-redirect" title="County of itself">county of itself</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-self57567_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-self57567-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sepNewc_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sepNewc-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-archivesMuseumSeparatedFromNorthumberland_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-archivesMuseumSeparatedFromNorthumberland-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-countyOfItself_Separated_1400_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-countyOfItself_Separated_1400-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> The city and the surrounding area created the new <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_county" title="Metropolitan county">metropolitan county</a> of <a href="/wiki/Tyne_and_Wear" title="Tyne and Wear">Tyne and Wear</a> in 1974.<sup id="cite_ref-countyOfItself_Separated_1400_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-countyOfItself_Separated_1400-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Newcastle is locally governed by <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_City_Council" title="Newcastle City Council">Newcastle City Council</a>.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" class="toclevel-2 tocsection-13"><a href="#Climate"><span class="tocnumber">2.5</span> <span class="toctext">Climate</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-14"><a href="#Environment"><span class="tocnumber">2.6</span> <span class="toctext">Environment</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-15"><a href="#Culture"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Culture</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-16"><a href="#Nightlife"><span class="tocnumber">3.1</span> <span class="toctext">Nightlife</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-17"><a href="#Food"><span class="tocnumber">3.2</span> <span class="toctext">Food</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-18"><a href="#Theatre"><span class="tocnumber">3.3</span> <span class="toctext">Theatre</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-19"><a href="#Literature_and_libraries"><span class="tocnumber">3.4</span> <span class="toctext">Literature and libraries</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-20"><a href="#Festivals_and_fairs"><span class="tocnumber">3.5</span> <span class="toctext">Festivals and fairs</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-21"><a href="#Music"><span class="tocnumber">3.6</span> <span class="toctext">Music</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-22"><a href="#Concert_venues"><span class="tocnumber">3.7</span> <span class="toctext">Concert venues</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-23"><a href="#Independent_Cinema"><span class="tocnumber">3.8</span> <span class="toctext">Independent Cinema</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-24"><a href="#Museums_and_galleries"><span class="tocnumber">3.9</span> <span class="toctext">Museums and galleries</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-25"><a href="#TV_and_film"><span class="tocnumber">3.10</span> <span class="toctext">TV and film</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-26"><a href="#Economy"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Economy</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-27"><a href="#Retail"><span class="tocnumber">4.1</span> <span class="toctext">Retail</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-28"><a href="#Population"><span class="tocnumber">5</span> <span class="toctext">Population</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-29"><a href="#Demographics"><span class="tocnumber">5.1</span> <span class="toctext">Demographics</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-30"><a href="#Age"><span class="tocnumber">5.1.1</span> <span class="toctext">Age</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-31"><a href="#Religion"><span class="tocnumber">5.1.2</span> <span class="toctext">Religion</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-32"><a href="#Ethnicity_and_nationality"><span class="tocnumber">5.1.3</span> <span class="toctext">Ethnicity and nationality</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-33"><a href="#Geordies"><span class="tocnumber">5.2</span> <span class="toctext">Geordies</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-34"><a href="#Dialect"><span class="tocnumber">5.2.1</span> <span class="toctext">Dialect</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-35"><a href="#Health"><span class="tocnumber">5.3</span> <span class="toctext">Health</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-36"><a href="#Sport"><span class="tocnumber">6</span> <span class="toctext">Sport</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-37"><a href="#Transport"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">Transport</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-38"><a href="#Air"><span class="tocnumber">7.1</span> <span class="toctext">Air</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-39"><a href="#Rail"><span class="tocnumber">7.2</span> <span class="toctext">Rail</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-40"><a href="#Metro"><span class="tocnumber">7.3</span> <span class="toctext">Metro</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2
